#### 4-year Plan
event = {
	id = 9300001
	country = GER
	random = no

	decision = { atwar = no ideology = nazi or = { event = 2003135 year = 1937 } } # Unemployment down to 5%
	decision_trigger = { money = 1000 minister = 58 } # Goering as MoA
	trigger = { or = { event = 2003135 year = 1937 } atwar = no ideology = nazi random = 50 }

	name = "9300001name"
	desc = "9300001desc"
	style = 2
	picture = "Four_Year"
	decision_picture = "decision_four_year"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 180
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }
	
	action = {
		ai_chance = 20
		name = "9300001a"
		command = { type = building_prod_mod which = ic value = 10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 5200 } } type = gain_tech which = 5200 } # Oil Refining 1938
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 5210 } } type = gain_tech which = 5210 } # Oil Refining 1940
		command = { type = domestic which = free_market value = -1 } # Autarky
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -1000 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = local_setflag which = GERAIIndustry }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = money value = -100 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = add_brigade value = super_heavy_artillery }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = add_brigade value = super_heavy_artillery }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = fort_attack which = super_heavy_artillery value = 6 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 60
		name = "9300001b"
    		command = { type = build_time which = armor when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
      		command = { type = build_time which = light_armor when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2650 } } type = gain_tech which = 2650 } # L ARM 1934
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2030 } } type = gain_tech which = 2030 } # L ARM 1936
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2040 } } type = gain_tech which = 2040 } # L ARM 1938
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2050 } } type = gain_tech which = 2050 } # L ARM 1939
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 2070 } } type = gain_tech which = 2070 } # ARM 1939
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -2000 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = local_setflag which = GERAIPanzers }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes } type = money value = -100 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 15
		name = "9300001c"
      		command = { type = build_time which = air when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -10 }
			command = { type = build_time which = paratrooper when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -5 }
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4400 } } type = gain_tech which = 4400 } # CAS 1934
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4170 } } type = gain_tech which = 4170 } # CAS 1937
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4280 } } type = gain_tech which = 4280 } # CAS 1940
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 4140 } } type = gain_tech which = 4140 } # TAC 1938
	   	command = { trigger = { NOT = { technology = 1670 } } type = gain_tech which = 1670 } # Airborne 1938

		alliance = { country = GER country = ROM }
		OR = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		ai = ROM
	}
	decision_trigger = { 
        	garrison = { country = GER province = 316 type = land size = 3 } # Bucarest
        	garrison = { country = GER province = 311 type = land size = 3 } # Ploesti
        	garrison = { country = GER province = 291 type = land size = 3 } # Sibiu
	}
	trigger = { 
		NOT = { ispuppet = ROM }
		alliance = { country = GER country = ROM }
		OR = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		random = 40
		OR = {
			AND = {
			garrison = { country = GER province = 316 type = land size = 3 } # Bucarest
        	garrison = { country = GER province = 311 type = land size = 3 } # Ploesti
        	garrison = { country = GER province = 291 type = land size = 3 } # Sibiu
			}
		land_percentage = { country = ROM value = 5.0 }	
		}
		event = 2003047 # German diplomatic offensive
		NOT = { oil = 1000 }
		OR = {
			NOT = { relation = { which = ROM value = 150 } }
			NOT = { lost_national = { country = SOV value = 15 } }
			}
		AND = {
			control = { province = 622 data = GER } #Three provinces onwards from Odessa - let's make sure ROM doesn't control too much, because if they do - this gives those provinces back to SOV...
			control = { province = 615 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 612 data = GER }
		}
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1945 }

# Align Portugal
event = {
	id = 9300175
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		event = 2003047 # German diplomatic offensive
		exists = POR
		alliance = { country = SPA country = GER }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = POR country = ENG } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = GER } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = ITA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = POR country = SPA } }
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } }
		alliance = { country = SPA country = GER }
		control = { province = 348 data = -3 }	# Gibraltar
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 453 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Caceres
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 450 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Plasencia
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 447 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Salamanca
		garrison = { country = -3 province = 458 type = land size = 1 area = 1 }  # Badajoz
}
	trigger = {
		alliance = { country = SPA country = GER }
		random = 20
		exists = POR
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }

# Form 'Volksgrenadier' Divisions
event = {
	id = 9300457
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { atwar = yes lost_national = { country = GER value = 5 } }

	decision_trigger = {
		event = 9300153 # Total War Speech
	}
	trigger = { 
	OR = {
		lost_national = { country = GER value = 25 }
		AND = {
			NOT = { land_percentage = { country = SOV value = 0.6 } }
			war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
			lost_national = { country = GER value = 5 }
			}
		}
		atwar = yes
		random = 50
	}
   
	name = 9300457name
	desc = 9300457desc
	style = 2
	picture = "volksgrenadier"
	decision_picture = "decision_Volksgrenadier"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
	  	command = { type = morale which = infantry value = 10 }
	  	command = { type = soft_attack which = infantry value = -3 }
	  	command = { type = hard_attack which = infantry value = -1 }
	  	command = { type = manpower which = infantry when = on_upgrade value = -4 }
		command = { type = build_cost which = infantry when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -25 }
		command = { type = build_time which = infantry when = on_upgrade where = relative value = -25 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -1000 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes not = { difficulty = 3 } } type = build_division which = militia when = 2 cost = -3.0 } #Queue 6 divs on neutral and Axis-favoured difficulties
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes not = { difficulty = 3 } } type = build_division which = militia when = 2 cost = -3.0 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes not = { difficulty = 3 } } type = build_division which = militia when = 2 cost = -3.0 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes not = { difficulty = 3 } } type = build_division which = infantry when = 3 cost = -4.5 } #Queue 6 divs on neutral and Axis-favoured difficulties
		command = { trigger = { ai = yes not = { difficulty = 3 } } type = build_division which = infantry when = 3 cost = -4.5 } # the above is because AI will not actually try to train militia at all at this point
	}
}

# Allied Crete Garrison (AI)
event = {
	id = 9300466
	random = no
	country = ENG
	
	name = 9300466name
	desc = 9300466desc

	trigger = { 
		atwar = yes
		ai = yes
		AND = {
			not = { ai = GER }
			exists = GER
			}
		control = { province = 382 data = ENG } # Irakleon
		random = 50
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		command = { type = activate_division which = 12700 value = 10040 where = 382 when = 0 } # Irakleon
	}
}

# Secret Intervention in Spain
event = {
	id = 9300467
	random = no
	tag = { ENG FRA }
	persistent = yes

	decision = {
		war = { country = SPA country = SPR }
		event = 2052002 #SPA fascist nation
		atwar = no
		NOT = {
			alliance = { country = FRA country = SPR }
			alliance = { country = ENG country = SPR }
			government = fascist
		}
		OR = { 
			NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_1 }
			NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_2 }
			NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_3 }
			NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_4 }
			NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_5 }
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = { 
			AND = { country = ENG NOT = { event = 2001026 } } # UK intervention
			AND = { country = FRA NOT = { event = 2002002 } } # FR intervention
		}
	}
	trigger = { ai = no }
   
	name = 9300467name
	desc = 9300467desc
	style = 2
	picture = "eng_fra_intervention"
	decision_picture = "decision_eng_fra_intervention"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 60
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		trigger = {
		supplies = 1000
		oil = 1000
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_1 }
		}
		name = 9300467a # Send humanitarian aid
		command = { type = supplies value = -1000 }
		command = { type = oilpool value = -1000 }
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 10 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300468 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_1 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = {
		supplies = 5000
		local_flag = Secret_SCW_1
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_2 }
		}
		name = 9300467b # Send weapons
		command = { type = supplies value = -5000 }
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 20 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300469 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_2 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = {
		manpower = 20
		local_flag = Secret_SCW_2
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_3 }
		}
		name = 9300467c # Send volunteers
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = -20 }
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 40 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300470 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_3 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = {
		manpower = 20
		local_flag = Secret_SCW_3
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_4 }
		}
		name = 9300467d # Send military advisers
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = -2 }
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 60 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300471 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_4 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = {
		country = ENG
		local_flag = Secret_SCW_4
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_5 }
		}
		name = 9300467e # Send army divisions
		command = { type = remove_division which = 12700 value = 1501 } # 49th (West Riding) Division
		command = { type = remove_division which = 12700 value = 511 } # 9th (Highland) Division
		command = { type = remove_division which = 12700 value = 517 } # 55th (West Lancashire) Division
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 100 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300472 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_5 }
	}
	action = {
		trigger = {
		country = FRA
		local_flag = Secret_SCW_4
		NOT = { local_flag = Secret_SCW_5 }
		}
		name = 9300467e # Send army divisions
		command = { type = remove_division which = 13500 value = 55 } # 21eme DI
		command = { type = remove_division which = 13500 value = 61 } # 12eme DIM
		command = { type = remove_division which = 13500 value = 32 } # 45eme DI
		command = { type = relation which = SPR value = 100 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 9300472 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = Secret_SCW_5 }
	}
}

		NOT = { exists = U45 }
		control = { province = 483 } # Oslo
	}	
	decision_trigger = { 
		money = 50
	}	
	trigger = { 
		#ai = no
		#event = 2003067 # Fall Weserübung		#Commented out in case player manually declares war on Norway
		event = 9300496 # Quisling
		NOT = { exists = NOR }
		NOT = { exists = U45 }
		control = { province = 483 } # Oslo
	}	

   	name = 9300497name

		command = { trigger = { ai = GER } type = activate_division which = 14500 value = 2108 where = 485 when = 0 } #Activate GAR division to help AI defend beaches

	id = 9300500
	random = no
	country = ENG

	decision = { 
			war = { country = GER } 
			event = 9300351 # Operation Seelowe
			control = { province = 55 data = -2 } # Paris
			control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
			not = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } } 
		}
	decision_trigger = { supplies = 1000 manpower = 60 }
	trigger = { 
			war = { country = GER } 
			event = 9300351 # Operation Seelowe
			control = { province = 55 data = -2 } # Paris
			control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
			not = { war = { country = SOV } } 
	}

	date = { year = 1933 month = january day = 1 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { year = 1999 month = december day = 29 }

   	name = 9300500name
	desc = 9300500desc
	style = 2
	picture = "home_guard"
	decision_picture = "decision_home_guard"

	action = {

		command = { type = build_division which = militia when = 1 cost = 0.1 name = "1st Home Guard" where = 10 }

# Implement Peking Plan
event = {
	id = 9300511
	random = no
	country = ENG

	decision = { 
			event = 2003024 # Ribbentrop-Molotov Pact
			atwar = no
			NOT = { atwar = POL }
			exists = POL
			control = { province = 232 data = POL } # Warsaw
			control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
			guarantee = { country = -1 country = POL }
		}
	decision_trigger = { supplies = 500 division_exists = { type = 18600 id = 64 } } # POL DD
	trigger = { 
			event = 2003024 # Ribbentrop-Molotov Pact
			atwar = no
			NOT = { atwar = POL }
			exists = POL
			control = { province = 232 data = POL } # Warsaw
			control = { province = 29 data = -3 } # London
			guarantee = { country = -1 country = POL }
			division_exists = { type = 18600 id = 64 } # POL DD
	}

	date = { year = 1933 month = january day = 1 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { year = 1999 month = december day = 29 }

   	name = 9300511name
	desc = 9300511desc
	style = 2
	decision_picture = "decision_opertion_peking"
	picture = "operation_peking"

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_GREAT
		command = { type = remove_division which = 18600 value = 64 }
		command = { type = add_division value = destroyer when = 4 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -500 }
	}
}
